The attitude of the staff here is pretty good, they ask for towels and toiletries, and the staff can deliver them to the big Hanyue building quickly.

There is a trolley pick up and drop off to the main station, the breakfast is also good, the entire hotel environment is superb, speechless, all scenery.

Next time I come, I think I will still live in Hanyuelou Insurance. In the Shoushan suite on the fifth floor, I can see the statue of Ksitigarbha. It is very beautiful.
